URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS1064059019	2021-02-01 15:41:23.103421	8110	species	Barn Owl	Tyto alba			1				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Washoe	US-NV-031	US-NV_1107	9			Swan Lake Nature Study Area (IBA)--Boardwalk	L3572935	H	39.6531916	-119.8564960	2021-01-30	15:03:00	obsr1242188	S80159954	Traveling	P22	EBIRD	84	1.014		1	1		0	1	0			I originally thought I had observed a short-eared owl.  Part of my reasoning stemmed from the Sibley guide stating that barn owls are "strictly nocturnal." My observation of this owl hunting and catching a rodent occurred in full sun in late afternoon. I subsequently studied online photographs of short-eared owls and barn owls, and I reviewed eBird records and photos for Swan Lake Natural Study Area.  I now realize that I observed a barn owl.  First, the owl flew directly toward me and I had a good view of its face, and I did not see black triangles extending to the sides of the eyes.  The facial disk was more uniformly tan/white.  Second, the owl I observed had golden tan coloring above, whereas short-eared owls are more chocolate brown above.
